18-20 Point Standard Decklists
==============================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on October 18, 2015 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/wizards_authorpic_larger.jpg)
By Wizards of the Coast










A total of 52 players earned 18-20 points from their Standard rounds at Pro Tour *Battle for Zendikar*, with 42 of those players finishing with 18 points (6-3), six grabbing an extra point to finish with 19 (6-2-1), and four players finishing with 20 points (6-1-2) thanks to multiple draws.




---

The following players finished with 20 points (6-1-2) in Standard:







#### Patrick Chapin


##### 




[![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)](/en/decklist/deck-list-ff9de2a1b0b34f409e0f964090f707e9?n=Patrick%20Chapin)
